 The software engineer of Indian origin has been awarded the Pulitzer Prize of the international newspaper 'the Wall Street Journal' for investigative reporting
 vah is puraskaar ke saajha vijeta hai
 According to Michael Cicconolfi, investigative editor of The Wall Street Journal, Palani Kumman is a software architect and technical chief at Dow Jones, the organization that publishes the newspaper
 palani vijayi project kii graphics team kaa hissaa hai
 The newspaper won the top journalism award for its comprehensive investigation project 'medicare Unmasked'
 isaki ghoshnaa somvaar ko hui
 The project included data collected from the US government after a long legal battle
 samachaarpatr ke lekhon ne chikitsa jagat main vyaapt dhokhadhadi evam kareeb 4
 Exposed wastage of government health insurance program covering 3 crore senior citizens and about 90 lakh people with severe disability

 Palani is a graduate of PSG College of Technology, Coimbatore, Tamil Nadu
